pregunta: 
echo "=== SO / HOST ==="
uname -a
cat /etc/os-release
hostname -f

echo "=== WEB SERVER ==="
sudo systemctl status nginx --no-pager || true
sudo systemctl status apache2 --no-pager || true
sudo systemctl status httpd --no-pager || true
ps aux | egrep 'nginx|apache2|httpd|php-fpm' | grep -v grep

echo "=== VHOSTS / CONFIG ==="
sudo nginx -T 2>/dev/null | sed -n '1,220p' || true
sudo apachectl -S 2>/dev/null || true
sudo httpd -S 2>/dev/null || true
sudo grep -R "DocumentRoot\\|server_name\\|ProxyPass\\|fastcgi_pass\\|php" /etc/nginx /etc/apache2 /etc/httpd 2>/dev/null | head -200

echo "=== PHP ==="
php -v || true
php -m | egrep 'pdo|pgsql|mysqli|curl|mbstring|json|openssl' || true
php-fpm -v 2>/dev/null || true

echo "=== RUTAS PUBLICAS ==="
sudo find /var/www -maxdepth 4 -type d 2>/dev/null | head -120
sudo find / -maxdepth 4 -type d -name "servicio" 2>/dev/null | head -40
sudo find / -maxdepth 5 -name "historico.php" 2>/dev/null | head -40
sudo find / -maxdepth 5 -name "login2.php" 2>/dev/null | head -40
